InterfaceIndex ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
    DISPLAY-HINT "d"
    STATUS       current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface or
            interface sub-layer in the managed system.  It is
            recommended that values are assigned contiguously starting
            from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer must remain
            constant at least from one re-initialization of the entity's
            network management system to the next re-initialization."
    SYNTAX       Integer32 (1..2147483647)

slot1ModuleIfEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot1ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry containing management information applicable to a
            particular interface."
    INDEX   { slot1ModuleifIndex }
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfTable 1 }
    
Slot1ModuleIfEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {
        slot1ModuleifIndex                 InterfaceIndex,  
        slot1ModuleIfId                    DisplayString,  
        slot1ModuleifDescr                 DisplayString,           
        slot1ModuleifType                  IANAifType,   		
        slot1ModuleifMtu                   Integer32,                
        slot1ModuleifSpeed                 Counter64,               
        slot1ModuleifPhysAddress           PhysAddress,              
        slot1ModuleifAdminStatus           INTEGER,                  
        slot1ModuleifOperStatus            INTEGER,                  
        slot1ModuleifLastChange            TimeTicks,                
        slot1ModuleifInOctets              Counter64,                
        slot1ModuleifInUcastPkts           Counter64,                
        slot1ModuleifInNUcastPkts          Counter64,  
        slot1ModuleifInDiscards            Counter64,
        slot1ModuleifInErrors              Counter64,
        slot1ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts        Counter64,
        slot1ModuleifInUnknownProtos       Counter64,	-- deprecated
        slot1ModuleifOutOctets             Counter64,
        slot1ModuleifOutUcastPkts          Counter64,
        slot1ModuleifOutNUcastPkts         Counter64,  -- deprecated
        slot1ModuleifOutDiscards           Counter64,
        slot1ModuleifOutErrors             Counter64,
        slot1ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts       Counter64,
        slot1ModuleifOutQLen               Gauge32,    -- deprecated  
        slot1ModuleifOutOctetsRate         Counter64,
        slot1ModuleifInOctetsRate          Counter64,
        slot1ModuleifOutPktsRate           Counter64,
        slot1ModuleifInPktsRate            Counter64,
        slot1ModuleifRxPower               DisplayString,
        slot1ModuleifTxPower               DisplayString,
        slot1ModuleifSpecific              OBJECT IDENTIFIER,
        slot1ModuleifTxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot1ModuleifRxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot1ModuleifRxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot1ModuleifRxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot1ModuleifTxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot1ModuleifTxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot1ModuleifRxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot1ModuleifTxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot1ModuleifMode                 DisplayString    		
    }         

slot1ModuleifIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface.  It
            is recommended that values are assigned contiguously
            starting from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer
            must remain constant at least from one re-initialization of
            the entity's network management system to the next re-
            initialization."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 1 }
    
slot1ModuleIfId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 2 }
    
slot1ModuleifDescr OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A textual string containing information about the
            interface.  This string should include the name of the
            manufacturer, the product name and the version of the
            interface hardware/software."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 3 }
    
slot1ModuleifType OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      IANAifType
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot1ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot1ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot1ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot1ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot1ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot1ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 10 }

slot1ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 11 }

slot1ModuleifInUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were not addressed to a multicast
            or broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 12 }

slot1ModuleifInNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were addressed to a multicast or
            broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifInMulticastPkts and
            ifInBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 13 }

slot1ModuleifInDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of inbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent

            their being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  One
            possible reason for discarding such a packet could be to
            free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 14 }

slot1ModuleifInErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of inbound
            packets that contained errors preventing them from being
            deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  For character-
            oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the number of inbound
            transmission units that contained errors preventing them
            from being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 15 }

slot1ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 16 }

slot1ModuleifInUnknownProtos OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of packets
            received via the interface which were discarded because of
            an unknown or unsupported protocol.  For character-oriented
            or fixed-length interfaces that support protocol
            multiplexing the number of transmission units received via
            the interface which were discarded because of an unknown or
            unsupported protocol.  For any interface that does not
            support protocol multiplexing, this counter will always be
            0.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 17 }

slot1ModuleifOutOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets transmitted out of the
            interface, including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 18 }

slot1ModuleifOutUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were not addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 19 }

slot1ModuleifOutNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifOutMulticastPkts
            and ifOutBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 20 }

slot1ModuleifOutDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of outbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent
            their being transmitted.  One possible reason for discarding
            such a packet could be to free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 21 }

slot1ModuleifOutErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of outbound
            packets that could not be transmitted because of errors.
            For character-oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the
            number of outbound transmission units that could not be
            transmitted because of errors.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 22 }

slot1ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 23 }

slot1ModuleifOutQLen OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Gauge32
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The length of the output packet queue (in packets)."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 24 }

slot1ModuleifOutOctetsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only

    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets trans on the interface(kbps)"

            "The speed of octets received on the interface(kbps)"
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 28 }

slot1ModuleifRxPower OBJECT-TYPE

    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 30 }

slot1ModuleifSpecific OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      OBJECT IDENTIFIER
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "A reference to MIB definitions specific to the particular
            media being used to realize the interface.  It is

            recommended that this value point to an instance of a MIB
            object in the media-specific MIB, i.e., that this object
            have the semantics associated with the InstancePointer
            textual convention defined in RFC 2579.  In fact, it is
            recommended that the media-specific MIB specify what value
            ifSpecific should/can take for values of ifType.  If no MIB
            definitions specific to the particular media are available,
            the value should be set to the OBJECT IDENTIFIER { 0 0 }."
    ::= { slot1ModuleIfEntry 31 }

-- slot 2 --

-- slot2Table --

slot2Table OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot2Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot2Type's utilization."
    ::= { slot2 1 }  

slot2Entry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot2Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot2's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot2Index }
    ::= { slot2Table 1 }

Slot2Entry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot2Index                       Integer32,
		slot2Type                        DisplayString,
		slot2Status                      DisplayString,		
        slot2SerialNumber                DisplayString,		
        slot2Temperature                 DisplayString
    }  

slot2Index OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot2."
    ::= { slot2Entry 1 }

slot2Type OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the slot2Type of each chassis."
    ::= { slot2Entry 2 }

slot2Status OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board status." 
    ::= { slot2Entry 3 }   

slot2SerialNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board serial number." 
    ::= { slot2Entry 4 }   

slot2Temperature OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board temperature." 
    ::= { slot2Entry 5 }   


slot2Module OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { slot2 2 }

-- slot2ModuleTable --
slot2ModuleTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot2ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot2Module's utilization."
    ::= { slot2Module 1 }  

slot2ModuleEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot2ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot2Module's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot2ModuleIndex }
    ::= { slot2ModuleTable 1 }

Slot2ModuleEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot2ModuleIndex                       Integer32,
		slot2ModuleId                           DisplayString,  
		slot2ModuleIfNumber                     Integer32		
    } 

slot2ModuleIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot2."
    ::= { slot2ModuleEntry 1 }

slot2ModuleId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot2ModuleEntry 2 }
  
slot2ModuleIfNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(0..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of network interfaces (regardless of their
            current state) present on this system." 
    ::= { slot2ModuleEntry 3 } 
    
slot2ModuleIfTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot2ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of interface entries.  The number of entries is
            given by the value of ifNumber."
    ::= { slot2Module 2 } 
    
slot2ModuleIfEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot2ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry containing management information applicable to a
            particular interface."
    INDEX   { slot2ModuleifIndex }
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfTable 1 }
    
Slot2ModuleIfEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {
        slot2ModuleifIndex                 InterfaceIndex,  
        slot2ModuleIfId                    DisplayString,  
        slot2ModuleifDescr                 DisplayString,           
        slot2ModuleifType                  IANAifType,   		
        slot2ModuleifMtu                   Integer32,                
        slot2ModuleifSpeed                 Counter64,               
        slot2ModuleifPhysAddress           PhysAddress,              
        slot2ModuleifAdminStatus           INTEGER,                  
        slot2ModuleifOperStatus            INTEGER,                  
        slot2ModuleifLastChange            TimeTicks,                
        slot2ModuleifInOctets              Counter64,                
        slot2ModuleifInUcastPkts           Counter64,                
        slot2ModuleifInNUcastPkts          Counter64,   
        slot2ModuleifInDiscards            Counter64,
        slot2ModuleifInErrors              Counter64,
        slot2ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts        Counter64,
        slot2ModuleifInUnknownProtos       Counter64,	-- deprecated
        slot2ModuleifOutOctets             Counter64,
        slot2ModuleifOutUcastPkts          Counter64,
        slot2ModuleifOutNUcastPkts         Counter64,  -- deprecated
        slot2ModuleifOutDiscards           Counter64,
        slot2ModuleifOutErrors             Counter64,
        slot2ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts       Counter64,
        slot2ModuleifOutQLen               Gauge32,    -- deprecated  
        slot2ModuleifOutOctetsRate         Counter64,
        slot2ModuleifInOctetsRate          Counter64,
        slot2ModuleifOutPktsRate           Counter64,
        slot2ModuleifInPktsRate            Counter64,
        slot2ModuleifRxPower               DisplayString,
        slot2ModuleifTxPower               DisplayString,
        slot2ModuleifSpecific              OBJECT IDENTIFIER,
        slot2ModuleifTxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot2ModuleifRxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot2ModuleifRxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot2ModuleifRxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot2ModuleifTxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot2ModuleifTxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot2ModuleifRxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot2ModuleifTxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot2ModuleifMode                 DisplayString   		
    }         

slot2ModuleifIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface.  It
            is recommended that values are assigned contiguously
            starting from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer
            must remain constant at least from one re-initialization of
            the entity's network management system to the next re-
            initialization."
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 1 }
    
slot2ModuleIfId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 2 }
    
slot2ModuleifDescr OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A textual string containing information about the
            interface.  This string should include the name of the
            manufacturer, the product name and the version of the
            interface hardware/software."
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 3 }
    
slot2ModuleifType OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      IANAifType
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot2ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot2ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot2ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot2ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot2ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot2ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 10 }

slot2ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 11 }

slot2ModuleifInUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were not addressed to a multicast

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other

            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 12 }

    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 13 }

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 21 }

slot2ModuleifOutErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of outbound
            packets that could not be transmitted because of errors.
            For character-oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the
            number of outbound transmission units that could not be
            transmitted because of errors.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 22 }

    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 23 }

    DESCRIPTION
            "The length of the output packet queue (in packets)."
    ::= { slot2ModuleIfEntry 24 }

slot2ModuleifSpecific OBJECT-TYPE

    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "A reference to MIB definitions specific to the particular
            media being used to realize the interface.  It is

            recommended that this value point to an instance of a MIB
            object in the media-specific MIB, i.e., that this object
            have the semantics associated with the InstancePointer
            textual convention defined in RFC 2579.  In fact, it is
            recommended that the media-specific MIB specify what value

            the value should be set to the OBJECT IDENTIFIER { 0 0 }."

-- slot 3 --

-- slot3Table --

slot3Table OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot3Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot3Type's utilization."
    ::= { slot3 1 }  

slot3Entry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot3Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot3's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot3Index }
    ::= { slot3Table 1 }

Slot3Entry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot3Index                       Integer32,
		slot3Type                        DisplayString,
		slot3Status                      DisplayString,		
        slot3SerialNumber                DisplayString,		
        slot3Temperature                 DisplayString
    }  

slot3Index OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot3."
    ::= { slot3Entry 1 }

slot3Type OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the slot3Type of each chassis."
    ::= { slot3Entry 2 }

slot3Status OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board status." 
    ::= { slot3Entry 3 }   


slot3SerialNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board serial number." 
    ::= { slot3Entry 4 }   

slot3Temperature OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board temperature." 
    ::= { slot3Entry 5 }   


slot3Module OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { slot3 2 }

-- slot3ModuleTable --
slot3ModuleTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot3ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot3Module's utilization."
    ::= { slot3Module 1 }  

slot3ModuleEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot3ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot3Module's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot3ModuleIndex }
    ::= { slot3ModuleTable 1 }

Slot3ModuleEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot3ModuleIndex                       Integer32,
		slot3ModuleId                           DisplayString,  
		slot3ModuleIfNumber                     Integer32		
    } 

slot3ModuleIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot3."
    ::= { slot3ModuleEntry 1 }

slot3ModuleId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot3ModuleEntry 2 }
  
slot3ModuleIfNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(0..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of network interfaces (regardless of their
            current state) present on this system." 
    ::= { slot3ModuleEntry 3 } 
    
slot3ModuleIfTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot3ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of interface entries.  The number of entries is
            given by the value of ifNumber."
    ::= { slot3Module 2 } 
    
slot3ModuleIfEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot3ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry containing management information applicable to a
            particular interface."
    INDEX   { slot3ModuleifIndex }
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfTable 1 }
    
Slot3ModuleIfEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {
        slot3ModuleifIndex                 InterfaceIndex,  
        slot3ModuleIfId                    DisplayString,  
        slot3ModuleifDescr                 DisplayString,           
        slot3ModuleifType                  IANAifType,   		
        slot3ModuleifMtu                   Integer32,                
        slot3ModuleifSpeed                 Counter64,               
        slot3ModuleifPhysAddress           PhysAddress,              
        slot3ModuleifAdminStatus           INTEGER,                  
        slot3ModuleifOperStatus            INTEGER,                  
        slot3ModuleifLastChange            TimeTicks,                
        slot3ModuleifInOctets              Counter64,                
        slot3ModuleifInUcastPkts           Counter64,                
        slot3ModuleifInNUcastPkts          Counter64,    
        slot3ModuleifInDiscards            Counter64,
        slot3ModuleifInErrors              Counter64,
        slot3ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts        Counter64,
        slot3ModuleifInUnknownProtos       Counter64,	-- deprecated
        slot3ModuleifOutOctets             Counter64,
        slot3ModuleifOutUcastPkts          Counter64,
        slot3ModuleifOutNUcastPkts         Counter64,  -- deprecated
        slot3ModuleifOutDiscards           Counter64,
        slot3ModuleifOutErrors             Counter64,
        slot3ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts       Counter64,
        slot3ModuleifOutQLen               Gauge32,    -- deprecated  
        slot3ModuleifOutOctetsRate         Counter64,
        slot3ModuleifInOctetsRate          Counter64,
        slot3ModuleifOutPktsRate           Counter64,
        slot3ModuleifInPktsRate            Counter64,
        slot3ModuleifRxPower               DisplayString,
        slot3ModuleifTxPower               DisplayString,
        slot3ModuleifSpecific              OBJECT IDENTIFIER,
        slot3ModuleifTxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot3ModuleifRxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot3ModuleifRxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot3ModuleifRxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot3ModuleifTxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot3ModuleifTxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot3ModuleifRxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot3ModuleifTxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot3ModuleifMode                 DisplayString   		
    }         

slot3ModuleifIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface.  It
            is recommended that values are assigned contiguously
            starting from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer
            must remain constant at least from one re-initialization of
            the entity's network management system to the next re-
            initialization."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 1 }
    
slot3ModuleIfId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 2 }
    
slot3ModuleifDescr OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A textual string containing information about the
            interface.  This string should include the name of the
            manufacturer, the product name and the version of the
            interface hardware/software."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 3 }
    
slot3ModuleifType OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      IANAifType
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot3ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot3ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot3ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot3ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot3ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot3ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 10 }

slot3ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 11 }

slot3ModuleifInUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were not addressed to a multicast
            or broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 12 }

slot3ModuleifInNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were addressed to a multicast or
            broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifInMulticastPkts and
            ifInBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 13 }

slot3ModuleifInDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of inbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent

            their being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  One
            possible reason for discarding such a packet could be to
            free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 14 }

slot3ModuleifInErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of inbound
            packets that contained errors preventing them from being
            deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  For character-
            oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the number of inbound
            transmission units that contained errors preventing them
            from being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 15 }

slot3ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 16 }

slot3ModuleifInUnknownProtos OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of packets
            received via the interface which were discarded because of
            an unknown or unsupported protocol.  For character-oriented
            or fixed-length interfaces that support protocol
            multiplexing the number of transmission units received via
            the interface which were discarded because of an unknown or
            unsupported protocol.  For any interface that does not
            support protocol multiplexing, this counter will always be
            0.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 17 }

slot3ModuleifOutOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets transmitted out of the
            interface, including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 18 }

slot3ModuleifOutUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were not addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 19 }

slot3ModuleifOutNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifOutMulticastPkts
            and ifOutBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 20 }

slot3ModuleifOutDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of outbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent
            their being transmitted.  One possible reason for discarding
            such a packet could be to free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 21 }

slot3ModuleifOutErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of outbound
            packets that could not be transmitted because of errors.
            For character-oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the
            number of outbound transmission units that could not be
            transmitted because of errors.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 22 }

slot3ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 23 }

slot3ModuleifOutQLen OBJECT-TYPE

    MAX-ACCESS  read-only

    DESCRIPTION
            "The length of the output packet queue (in packets)."
    ::= { slot3ModuleIfEntry 24 }

slot3ModuleifRxPowerMax OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION

slot4Module OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { slot4 2 }

-- slot4ModuleTable --
slot4ModuleTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot4ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot4Module's utilization."
    ::= { slot4Module 1 }  

slot4ModuleEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot4ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot4Module's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot4ModuleIndex }
    ::= { slot4ModuleTable 1 }

Slot4ModuleEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot4ModuleIndex                       Integer32,
		slot4ModuleId                           DisplayString,  
		slot4ModuleIfNumber                     Integer32		
    } 

slot4ModuleIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot4."
    ::= { slot4ModuleEntry 1 }

slot4ModuleId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot4ModuleEntry 2 }
  
slot4ModuleIfNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(0..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of network interfaces (regardless of their
            current state) present on this system." 
    ::= { slot4ModuleEntry 3 } 
    
slot4ModuleIfTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot4ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of interface entries.  The number of entries is
            given by the value of ifNumber."
    ::= { slot4Module 2 } 
    
slot4ModuleIfEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot4ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry containing management information applicable to a
            particular interface."
    INDEX   { slot4ModuleifIndex }
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfTable 1 }
    
Slot4ModuleIfEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {
        slot4ModuleifIndex                 InterfaceIndex,  
        slot4ModuleIfId                    DisplayString,  
        slot4ModuleifDescr                 DisplayString,           
        slot4ModuleifType                  IANAifType,   		
        slot4ModuleifMtu                   Integer32,                
        slot4ModuleifSpeed                 Counter64,               
        slot4ModuleifPhysAddress           PhysAddress,              
        slot4ModuleifAdminStatus           INTEGER,                  
        slot4ModuleifOperStatus            INTEGER,                  
        slot4ModuleifLastChange            TimeTicks,                
        slot4ModuleifInOctets              Counter64,                
        slot4ModuleifInUcastPkts           Counter64,                
        slot4ModuleifInNUcastPkts          Counter64,    
        slot4ModuleifInDiscards            Counter64,
        slot4ModuleifInErrors              Counter64,
        slot4ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts        Counter64,
        slot4ModuleifInUnknownProtos       Counter64,	-- deprecated
        slot4ModuleifOutOctets             Counter64,
        slot4ModuleifOutUcastPkts          Counter64,
        slot4ModuleifOutNUcastPkts         Counter64,  -- deprecated
        slot4ModuleifOutDiscards           Counter64,
        slot4ModuleifOutErrors             Counter64,
        slot4ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts       Counter64,
        slot4ModuleifOutQLen               Gauge32,    -- deprecated  
        slot4ModuleifOutOctetsRate         Counter64,
        slot4ModuleifInOctetsRate          Counter64,
        slot4ModuleifOutPktsRate           Counter64,
        slot4ModuleifInPktsRate            Counter64,
        slot4ModuleifRxPower               DisplayString,
        slot4ModuleifTxPower               DisplayString,
        slot4ModuleifSpecific              OBJECT IDENTIFIER,
        slot4ModuleifTxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot4ModuleifRxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot4ModuleifRxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot4ModuleifRxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot4ModuleifTxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot4ModuleifTxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot4ModuleifRxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot4ModuleifTxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot4ModuleifMode                 DisplayString   		
    }         

slot4ModuleifIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface.  It
            is recommended that values are assigned contiguously
            starting from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer
            must remain constant at least from one re-initialization of
            the entity's network management system to the next re-
            initialization."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 1 }
    
slot4ModuleIfId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 2 }
    
slot4ModuleifDescr OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A textual string containing information about the
            interface.  This string should include the name of the
            manufacturer, the product name and the version of the
            interface hardware/software."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 3 }
    
slot4ModuleifType OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      IANAifType
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot4ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot4ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot4ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot4ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot4ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot4ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 10 }

slot4ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 11 }

slot4ModuleifInUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were not addressed to a multicast
            or broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 12 }

slot4ModuleifInNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were addressed to a multicast or
            broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifInMulticastPkts and
            ifInBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 13 }

slot4ModuleifInDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of inbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent

            their being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  One
            possible reason for discarding such a packet could be to
            free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 14 }

slot4ModuleifInErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of inbound
            packets that contained errors preventing them from being
            deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  For character-
            oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the number of inbound
            transmission units that contained errors preventing them
            from being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 15 }

slot4ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 16 }

slot4ModuleifInUnknownProtos OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of packets
            received via the interface which were discarded because of
            an unknown or unsupported protocol.  For character-oriented
            or fixed-length interfaces that support protocol
            multiplexing the number of transmission units received via
            the interface which were discarded because of an unknown or
            unsupported protocol.  For any interface that does not
            support protocol multiplexing, this counter will always be
            0.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 17 }

slot4ModuleifOutOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets transmitted out of the
            interface, including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 18 }

slot4ModuleifOutUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were not addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 19 }

slot4ModuleifOutNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifOutMulticastPkts
            and ifOutBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 20 }

slot4ModuleifOutDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of outbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent
            their being transmitted.  One possible reason for discarding
            such a packet could be to free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 21 }

slot4ModuleifOutErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of outbound
            packets that could not be transmitted because of errors.
            For character-oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the
            number of outbound transmission units that could not be
            transmitted because of errors.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 22 }

slot4ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 23 }

slot4ModuleifOutQLen OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Gauge32
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The length of the output packet queue (in packets)."
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 24 }

slot4ModuleifOutOctetsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets trans on the interface(kbps)"
    ::= { slot4ModuleIfEntry 25 }

            media being used to realize the interface.  It is

            recommended that this value point to an instance of a MIB
            object in the media-specific MIB, i.e., that this object
            have the semantics associated with the InstancePointer
            textual convention defined in RFC 2579.  In fact, it is
            recommended that the media-specific MIB specify what value
            ifSpecific should/can take for values of ifType.  If no MIB
            definitions specific to the particular media are available,
            the value should be set to the OBJECT IDENTIFIER { 0 0 }."
