slot5ModuleIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot5."
    ::= { slot5ModuleEntry 1 }

slot5ModuleId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot5ModuleEntry 2 }
  
slot5ModuleIfNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(0..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of network interfaces (regardless of their
            current state) present on this system." 
    ::= { slot5ModuleEntry 3 } 
    
slot5ModuleIfTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot5ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of interface entries.  The number of entries is
            given by the value of ifNumber."
    ::= { slot5Module 2 } 
    
slot5ModuleIfEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot5ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry containing management information applicable to a
            particular interface."
    INDEX   { slot5ModuleifIndex }
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfTable 1 }
    
Slot5ModuleIfEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {
        slot5ModuleifIndex                 InterfaceIndex,  
        slot5ModuleIfId                    DisplayString,  
        slot5ModuleifDescr                 DisplayString,           
        slot5ModuleifType                  IANAifType,   		
        slot5ModuleifMtu                   Integer32,                
        slot5ModuleifSpeed                 Counter64,               
        slot5ModuleifPhysAddress           PhysAddress,              
        slot5ModuleifAdminStatus           INTEGER,                  
        slot5ModuleifOperStatus            INTEGER,                  
        slot5ModuleifLastChange            TimeTicks,                
        slot5ModuleifInOctets              Counter64,                
        slot5ModuleifInUcastPkts           Counter64,                
        slot5ModuleifInNUcastPkts          Counter64,  
        slot5ModuleifInDiscards            Counter64,
        slot5ModuleifInErrors              Counter64,
        slot5ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts        Counter64,
        slot5ModuleifInUnknownProtos       Counter64,	-- deprecated
        slot5ModuleifOutOctets             Counter64,
        slot5ModuleifOutUcastPkts          Counter64,
        slot5ModuleifOutNUcastPkts         Counter64,  -- deprecated
        slot5ModuleifOutDiscards           Counter64,
        slot5ModuleifOutErrors             Counter64,
        slot5ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts       Counter64,
        slot5ModuleifOutQLen               Gauge32,    -- deprecated  
        slot5ModuleifOutOctetsRate         Counter64,
        slot5ModuleifInOctetsRate          Counter64,
        slot5ModuleifOutPktsRate           Counter64,
        slot5ModuleifInPktsRate            Counter64,
        slot5ModuleifRxPower               DisplayString,
        slot5ModuleifTxPower               DisplayString,
        slot5ModuleifSpecific              OBJECT IDENTIFIER,
        slot5ModuleifTxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot5ModuleifRxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot5ModuleifRxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot5ModuleifRxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot5ModuleifTxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot5ModuleifTxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot5ModuleifRxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot5ModuleifTxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot5ModuleifMode                 DisplayString   		
    }         

slot5ModuleifIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface.  It
            is recommended that values are assigned contiguously
            starting from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer
            must remain constant at least from one re-initialization of
            the entity's network management system to the next re-
            initialization."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 1 }
    
slot5ModuleIfId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 2 }
    
slot5ModuleifDescr OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A textual string containing information about the
            interface.  This string should include the name of the
            manufacturer, the product name and the version of the
            interface hardware/software."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 3 }
    
slot5ModuleifType OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      IANAifType
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot5ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot5ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot5ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot5ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot5ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot5ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 10 }

slot5ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 11 }

slot5ModuleifInUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were not addressed to a multicast
            or broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 12 }

slot5ModuleifInNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were addressed to a multicast or
            broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifInMulticastPkts and
            ifInBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 13 }

slot5ModuleifInDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of inbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent

            their being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  One
            possible reason for discarding such a packet could be to
            free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 14 }

slot5ModuleifInErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of inbound
            packets that contained errors preventing them from being
            deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  For character-
            oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the number of inbound
            transmission units that contained errors preventing them
            from being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 15 }

slot5ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 16 }

slot5ModuleifInUnknownProtos OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of packets
            received via the interface which were discarded because of
            an unknown or unsupported protocol.  For character-oriented
            or fixed-length interfaces that support protocol
            multiplexing the number of transmission units received via
            the interface which were discarded because of an unknown or
            unsupported protocol.  For any interface that does not
            support protocol multiplexing, this counter will always be
            0.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 17 }

slot5ModuleifOutOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets transmitted out of the
            interface, including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 18 }

slot5ModuleifOutUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were not addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 19 }

slot5ModuleifOutNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifOutMulticastPkts
            and ifOutBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 20 }

slot5ModuleifOutDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of outbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent
            their being transmitted.  One possible reason for discarding
            such a packet could be to free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 21 }

slot5ModuleifOutErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of outbound
            packets that could not be transmitted because of errors.
            For character-oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the
            number of outbound transmission units that could not be
            transmitted because of errors.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 22 }

slot5ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 23 }

slot5ModuleifOutQLen OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Gauge32
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The length of the output packet queue (in packets)."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 24 }

slot5ModuleifOutOctetsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets trans on the interface(kbps)"
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 25 }

slot5ModuleifInOctetsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets received on the interface(kbps)"
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 26 }

    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of packets trans on the interface(pps)"
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 27 }

slot5ModuleifInPktsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets received on the interface(kbps)"
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 28 }

    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 30 }

slot5ModuleifSpecific OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      OBJECT IDENTIFIER
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "A reference to MIB definitions specific to the particular
            media being used to realize the interface.  It is

            recommended that this value point to an instance of a MIB
            object in the media-specific MIB, i.e., that this object
            have the semantics associated with the InstancePointer
            textual convention defined in RFC 2579.  In fact, it is
            recommended that the media-specific MIB specify what value
            ifSpecific should/can take for values of ifType.  If no MIB
            definitions specific to the particular media are available,
            the value should be set to the OBJECT IDENTIFIER { 0 0 }."
    ::= { slot5ModuleIfEntry 31 }

-- slot6Table --

slot6Table OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot6Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot6Type's utilization."
    ::= { slot6 1 }  

slot6Entry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot6Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot6's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot6Index }
    ::= { slot6Table 1 }

Slot6Entry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot6Index                       Integer32,
		slot6Type                        DisplayString,
		slot6Status                      DisplayString,		
        slot6SerialNumber                DisplayString,		
        slot6Temperature                 DisplayString
    }  

slot6Index OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot6."
    ::= { slot6Entry 1 }

slot6Type OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the slot6Type of each chassis."
    ::= { slot6Entry 2 }

slot6Status OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board status." 
    ::= { slot6Entry 3 }   


slot6SerialNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board serial number." 
    ::= { slot6Entry 4 }   

slot6Temperature OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board temperature." 
    ::= { slot6Entry 5 }   


slot6Module OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { slot6 2 }

    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot6ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot6ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot6ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot6ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot6ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot6ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 10 }

slot6ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 11 }

slot6ModuleifInUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were not addressed to a multicast
            or broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 12 }

slot6ModuleifInNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were addressed to a multicast or
            broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifInMulticastPkts and
            ifInBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 13 }

slot6ModuleifInDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of inbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent

            their being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  One
            possible reason for discarding such a packet could be to
            free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 14 }

slot6ModuleifInErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of inbound
            packets that contained errors preventing them from being
            deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  For character-
            oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the number of inbound
            transmission units that contained errors preventing them
            from being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 15 }

slot6ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 16 }

slot6ModuleifInUnknownProtos OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of packets
            received via the interface which were discarded because of
            an unknown or unsupported protocol.  For character-oriented
            or fixed-length interfaces that support protocol
            multiplexing the number of transmission units received via
            the interface which were discarded because of an unknown or
            unsupported protocol.  For any interface that does not
            support protocol multiplexing, this counter will always be
            0.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 17 }

slot6ModuleifOutOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets transmitted out of the
            interface, including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 18 }

slot6ModuleifOutUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were not addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 19 }

slot6ModuleifOutNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifOutMulticastPkts
            and ifOutBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 20 }

slot6ModuleifOutDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of outbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent
            their being transmitted.  One possible reason for discarding
            such a packet could be to free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 21 }

slot6ModuleifOutErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of outbound
            packets that could not be transmitted because of errors.
            For character-oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the
            number of outbound transmission units that could not be
            transmitted because of errors.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 22 }

slot6ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 23 }

slot6ModuleifOutQLen OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Gauge32
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The length of the output packet queue (in packets)."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 24 }

slot6ModuleifOutOctetsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets trans on the interface(kbps)"
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 25 }

            "The speed of packets trans on the interface(pps)"
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 27 }

            "The speed of octets received on the interface(kbps)"

slot6ModuleifSpecific OBJECT-TYPE

    MAX-ACCESS  read-only

    DESCRIPTION
            "A reference to MIB definitions specific to the particular
            media being used to realize the interface.  It is

            recommended that this value point to an instance of a MIB
            object in the media-specific MIB, i.e., that this object
            have the semantics associated with the InstancePointer
            textual convention defined in RFC 2579.  In fact, it is
            recommended that the media-specific MIB specify what value
            ifSpecific should/can take for values of ifType.  If no MIB
            definitions specific to the particular media are available,
            the value should be set to the OBJECT IDENTIFIER { 0 0 }."
    ::= { slot6ModuleIfEntry 31 }

-- slot 7 --

-- slot7Table --

slot7Table OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot7Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot7Type's utilization."
    ::= { slot7 1 }  

slot7Entry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot7Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot7's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot7Index }
    ::= { slot7Table 1 }

Slot7Entry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot7Index                       Integer32,
		slot7Type                        DisplayString,
		slot7Status                      DisplayString,		
        slot7SerialNumber                DisplayString,		
        slot7Temperature                 DisplayString
    }  

slot7Index OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot7."
    ::= { slot7Entry 1 }

slot7Type OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the slot7Type of each chassis."
    ::= { slot7Entry 2 }

slot7Status OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board status." 
    ::= { slot7Entry 3 }   


slot7SerialNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board serial number." 
    ::= { slot7Entry 4 }   

slot7Temperature OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board temperature." 
    ::= { slot7Entry 5 }   


slot7Module OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { slot7 2 }

-- slot7ModuleTable --
slot7ModuleTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot7ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot7Module's utilization."
    ::= { slot7Module 1 }  

slot7ModuleEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot7ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot7Module's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot7ModuleIndex }
    ::= { slot7ModuleTable 1 }

Slot7ModuleEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot7ModuleIndex                       Integer32,
		slot7ModuleId                           DisplayString,  
		slot7ModuleIfNumber                     Integer32		
    } 

slot7ModuleIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot7."
    ::= { slot7ModuleEntry 1 }

slot7ModuleId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot7ModuleEntry 2 }
  
slot7ModuleIfNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(0..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of network interfaces (regardless of their
            current state) present on this system." 
    ::= { slot7ModuleEntry 3 } 
    
slot7ModuleIfTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot7ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of interface entries.  The number of entries is
            given by the value of ifNumber."
    ::= { slot7Module 2 } 
    
slot7ModuleIfEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot7ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry containing management information applicable to a
            particular interface."
    INDEX   { slot7ModuleifIndex }
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfTable 1 }
    
Slot7ModuleIfEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {
        slot7ModuleifIndex                 InterfaceIndex,  
        slot7ModuleIfId                    DisplayString,  
        slot7ModuleifDescr                 DisplayString,           
        slot7ModuleifType                  IANAifType,   		
        slot7ModuleifMtu                   Integer32,                
        slot7ModuleifSpeed                 Counter64,               
        slot7ModuleifPhysAddress           PhysAddress,              
        slot7ModuleifAdminStatus           INTEGER,                  
        slot7ModuleifOperStatus            INTEGER,                  
        slot7ModuleifLastChange            TimeTicks,                
        slot7ModuleifInOctets              Counter64,                
        slot7ModuleifInUcastPkts           Counter64,                
        slot7ModuleifInNUcastPkts          Counter64,    
        slot7ModuleifInDiscards            Counter64,
        slot7ModuleifInErrors              Counter64,
        slot7ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts        Counter64,
        slot7ModuleifInUnknownProtos       Counter64,	-- deprecated
        slot7ModuleifOutOctets             Counter64,
        slot7ModuleifOutUcastPkts          Counter64,
        slot7ModuleifOutNUcastPkts         Counter64,  -- deprecated
        slot7ModuleifOutDiscards           Counter64,
        slot7ModuleifOutErrors             Counter64,
        slot7ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts       Counter64,
        slot7ModuleifOutQLen               Gauge32,    -- deprecated  
        slot7ModuleifOutOctetsRate         Counter64,
        slot7ModuleifInOctetsRate          Counter64,
        slot7ModuleifOutPktsRate           Counter64,
        slot7ModuleifInPktsRate            Counter64,
        slot7ModuleifRxPower               DisplayString,
        slot7ModuleifTxPower               DisplayString,
        slot7ModuleifSpecific              OBJECT IDENTIFIER,
        slot7ModuleifTxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot7ModuleifRxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot7ModuleifRxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot7ModuleifRxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot7ModuleifTxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot7ModuleifTxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot7ModuleifRxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot7ModuleifTxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot7ModuleifMode                 DisplayString   		
    }         

slot7ModuleifIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface.  It
            is recommended that values are assigned contiguously
            starting from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer
            must remain constant at least from one re-initialization of
            the entity's network management system to the next re-
            initialization."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 1 }
    
slot7ModuleIfId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 2 }
    
slot7ModuleifDescr OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A textual string containing information about the
            interface.  This string should include the name of the
            manufacturer, the product name and the version of the
            interface hardware/software."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 3 }
    
slot7ModuleifType OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      IANAifType
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot7ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot7ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot7ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot7ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot7ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot7ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 10 }

slot7ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 11 }

slot7ModuleifInUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were not addressed to a multicast
            or broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 12 }

slot7ModuleifInNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were addressed to a multicast or
            broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifInMulticastPkts and
            ifInBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 13 }

slot7ModuleifInDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of inbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent

            their being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  One
            possible reason for discarding such a packet could be to
            free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 14 }

slot7ModuleifInErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of inbound
            packets that contained errors preventing them from being
            deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  For character-
            oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the number of inbound
            transmission units that contained errors preventing them
            from being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 15 }

slot7ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 16 }

slot7ModuleifInUnknownProtos OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of packets
            received via the interface which were discarded because of
            an unknown or unsupported protocol.  For character-oriented
            or fixed-length interfaces that support protocol
            multiplexing the number of transmission units received via
            the interface which were discarded because of an unknown or
            unsupported protocol.  For any interface that does not
            support protocol multiplexing, this counter will always be
            0.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 17 }

slot7ModuleifOutOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets transmitted out of the
            interface, including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 18 }

slot7ModuleifOutUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were not addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 19 }

slot7ModuleifOutNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifOutMulticastPkts
            and ifOutBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 20 }

slot7ModuleifOutDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of outbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent
            their being transmitted.  One possible reason for discarding
            such a packet could be to free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 21 }

slot7ModuleifOutErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of outbound
            packets that could not be transmitted because of errors.
            For character-oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the
            number of outbound transmission units that could not be
            transmitted because of errors.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 22 }

slot7ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 23 }

slot7ModuleifOutQLen OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Gauge32
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The length of the output packet queue (in packets)."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 24 }

slot7ModuleifOutOctetsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only

    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets trans on the interface(kbps)"

    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 27 }

    MAX-ACCESS  read-only

    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets received on the interface(kbps)"
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 28 }

slot7ModuleifRxPower OBJECT-TYPE

    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 30 }

slot7ModuleifSpecific OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      OBJECT IDENTIFIER
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "A reference to MIB definitions specific to the particular
            media being used to realize the interface.  It is

            recommended that this value point to an instance of a MIB
            object in the media-specific MIB, i.e., that this object
            have the semantics associated with the InstancePointer
            textual convention defined in RFC 2579.  In fact, it is
            recommended that the media-specific MIB specify what value
            ifSpecific should/can take for values of ifType.  If no MIB
            definitions specific to the particular media are available,
            the value should be set to the OBJECT IDENTIFIER { 0 0 }."
    ::= { slot7ModuleIfEntry 31 }

-- slot 8 --

-- slot8Table --

slot8Table OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot8Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot8Type's utilization."
    ::= { slot8 1 }  

slot8Entry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot8Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot8's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot8Index }
    ::= { slot8Table 1 }

Slot8Entry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot8Index                       Integer32,
		slot8Type                        DisplayString,
		slot8Status                      DisplayString,		
        slot8SerialNumber                DisplayString,		
        slot8Temperature                 DisplayString
    }  

slot8Index OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot8."
    ::= { slot8Entry 1 }

slot8Type OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the slot8Type of each chassis."
    ::= { slot8Entry 2 }

slot8Status OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board status." 
    ::= { slot8Entry 3 }   


slot8SerialNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board serial number." 
    ::= { slot8Entry 4 }   

slot8Temperature OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board temperature." 
    ::= { slot8Entry 5 }   


slot8Module OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { slot8 2 }

-- slot8ModuleTable --
slot8ModuleTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot8ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot8Module's utilization."
    ::= { slot8Module 1 }  

slot8ModuleEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot8ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot8Module's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot8ModuleIndex }
    ::= { slot8ModuleTable 1 }

Slot8ModuleEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot8ModuleIndex                       Integer32,
		slot8ModuleId                           DisplayString,  
		slot8ModuleIfNumber                     Integer32		
    } 

slot8ModuleIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot8."
    ::= { slot8ModuleEntry 1 }

slot8ModuleId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot8ModuleEntry 2 }
  
slot8ModuleIfNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(0..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of network interfaces (regardless of their
            current state) present on this system." 
    ::= { slot8ModuleEntry 3 } 
    
slot8ModuleIfTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot8ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of interface entries.  The number of entries is
            given by the value of ifNumber."
    ::= { slot8Module 2 } 
    
slot8ModuleIfEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot8ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry containing management information applicable to a
            particular interface."
    INDEX   { slot8ModuleifIndex }
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfTable 1 }
    
Slot8ModuleIfEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {
        slot8ModuleifIndex                 InterfaceIndex,  
        slot8ModuleIfId                    DisplayString,  
        slot8ModuleifDescr                 DisplayString,           
        slot8ModuleifType                  IANAifType,   		
        slot8ModuleifMtu                   Integer32,                
        slot8ModuleifSpeed                 Counter64,               
        slot8ModuleifPhysAddress           PhysAddress,              
        slot8ModuleifAdminStatus           INTEGER,                  
        slot8ModuleifOperStatus            INTEGER,                  
        slot8ModuleifLastChange            TimeTicks,                
        slot8ModuleifInOctets              Counter64,                
        slot8ModuleifInUcastPkts           Counter64,                
        slot8ModuleifInNUcastPkts          Counter64,  
        slot8ModuleifInDiscards            Counter64,
        slot8ModuleifInErrors              Counter64,
        slot8ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts        Counter64,
        slot8ModuleifInUnknownProtos       Counter64,	-- deprecated
        slot8ModuleifOutOctets             Counter64,
        slot8ModuleifOutUcastPkts          Counter64,
        slot8ModuleifOutNUcastPkts         Counter64,  -- deprecated
        slot8ModuleifOutDiscards           Counter64,
        slot8ModuleifOutErrors             Counter64,
        slot8ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts       Counter64,
        slot8ModuleifOutQLen               Gauge32,    -- deprecated  
        slot8ModuleifOutOctetsRate         Counter64,
        slot8ModuleifInOctetsRate          Counter64,
        slot8ModuleifOutPktsRate           Counter64,
        slot8ModuleifInPktsRate            Counter64,
        slot8ModuleifRxPower               DisplayString,
        slot8ModuleifTxPower               DisplayString,
        slot8ModuleifSpecific              OBJECT IDENTIFIER,
        slot8ModuleifTxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot8ModuleifRxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot8ModuleifRxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot8ModuleifRxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot8ModuleifTxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot8ModuleifTxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot8ModuleifRxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot8ModuleifTxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot8ModuleifMode                 DisplayString   		
    }         

slot8ModuleifIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface.  It
            is recommended that values are assigned contiguously
            starting from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer
            must remain constant at least from one re-initialization of
            the entity's network management system to the next re-
            initialization."
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 1 }
    
slot8ModuleIfId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 2 }
    
slot8ModuleifDescr OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A textual string containing information about the
            interface.  This string should include the name of the
            manufacturer, the product name and the version of the
            interface hardware/software."
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 3 }
    
slot8ModuleifType OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      IANAifType
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot8ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot8ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot8ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot8ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot8ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot8ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 10 }

slot8ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 11 }

    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 19 }

slot8ModuleifOutNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifOutMulticastPkts
            and ifOutBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 20 }

    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of outbound packets which were chosen to be

            such a packet could be to free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 21 }

slot8ModuleifOutErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of outbound
            packets that could not be transmitted because of errors.
            For character-oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the
            number of outbound transmission units that could not be
            transmitted because of errors.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 22 }

    DESCRIPTION
            "A reference to MIB definitions specific to the particular
            media being used to realize the interface.  It is

            recommended that this value point to an instance of a MIB
            object in the media-specific MIB, i.e., that this object
            have the semantics associated with the InstancePointer
            textual convention defined in RFC 2579.  In fact, it is
            recommended that the media-specific MIB specify what value
            ifSpecific should/can take for values of ifType.  If no MIB
            definitions specific to the particular media are available,
            the value should be set to the OBJECT IDENTIFIER { 0 0 }."
    ::= { slot8ModuleIfEntry 31 }
