-- slot 9 --

-- slot9Table --

slot9Table OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot9Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot9Type's utilization."
    ::= { slot9 1 }  

slot9Entry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot9Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot9's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot9Index }
    ::= { slot9Table 1 }

Slot9Entry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot9Index                       Integer32,
		slot9Type                        DisplayString,
		slot9Status                      DisplayString,		
        slot9SerialNumber                DisplayString,		
        slot9Temperature                 DisplayString
    }  

slot9Index OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot9."
    ::= { slot9Entry 1 }

slot9Type OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the slot9Type of each chassis."
    ::= { slot9Entry 2 }

slot9Status OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board status." 
    ::= { slot9Entry 3 }   


slot9SerialNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board serial number." 
    ::= { slot9Entry 4 }   

slot9Temperature OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board temperature." 
    ::= { slot9Entry 5 }   


slot9Module OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { slot9 2 }

-- slot9ModuleTable --
slot9ModuleTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot9ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot9Module's utilization."
    ::= { slot9Module 1 }  

slot9ModuleEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot9ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot9Module's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot9ModuleIndex }
    ::= { slot9ModuleTable 1 }

Slot9ModuleEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot9ModuleIndex                       Integer32,
		slot9ModuleId                           DisplayString,  
		slot9ModuleIfNumber                     Integer32		
    } 

slot9ModuleIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot9."
    ::= { slot9ModuleEntry 1 }

slot9ModuleId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot9ModuleEntry 2 }
  
slot9ModuleIfNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(0..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of network interfaces (regardless of their
            current state) present on this system." 
    ::= { slot9ModuleEntry 3 } 
    
slot9ModuleIfTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot9ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of interface entries.  The number of entries is
            given by the value of ifNumber."
    ::= { slot9Module 2 } 
    
slot9ModuleIfEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot9ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry containing management information applicable to a
            particular interface."
    INDEX   { slot9ModuleifIndex }
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfTable 1 }
    
Slot9ModuleIfEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {
        slot9ModuleifIndex                 InterfaceIndex,  
        slot9ModuleIfId                    DisplayString,  
        slot9ModuleifDescr                 DisplayString,           
        slot9ModuleifType                  IANAifType,   		
        slot9ModuleifMtu                   Integer32,                
        slot9ModuleifSpeed                 Counter64,               
        slot9ModuleifPhysAddress           PhysAddress,              
        slot9ModuleifAdminStatus           INTEGER,                  
        slot9ModuleifOperStatus            INTEGER,                  
        slot9ModuleifLastChange            TimeTicks,                
        slot9ModuleifInOctets              Counter64,                
        slot9ModuleifInUcastPkts           Counter64,                
        slot9ModuleifInNUcastPkts          Counter64,   
        slot9ModuleifInDiscards            Counter64,
        slot9ModuleifInErrors              Counter64,
        slot9ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts        Counter64,
        slot9ModuleifInUnknownProtos       Counter64,	-- deprecated
        slot9ModuleifOutOctets             Counter64,
        slot9ModuleifOutUcastPkts          Counter64,
        slot9ModuleifOutNUcastPkts         Counter64,  -- deprecated
        slot9ModuleifOutDiscards           Counter64,
        slot9ModuleifOutErrors             Counter64,
        slot9ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts       Counter64,
        slot9ModuleifOutQLen               Gauge32,    -- deprecated  
        slot9ModuleifOutOctetsRate         Counter64,
        slot9ModuleifInOctetsRate          Counter64,
        slot9ModuleifOutPktsRate           Counter64,
        slot9ModuleifInPktsRate            Counter64,
        slot9ModuleifRxPower               DisplayString,
        slot9ModuleifTxPower               DisplayString,
        slot9ModuleifSpecific              OBJECT IDENTIFIER,
        slot9ModuleifTxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot9ModuleifRxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot9ModuleifRxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot9ModuleifRxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot9ModuleifTxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot9ModuleifTxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot9ModuleifRxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot9ModuleifTxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot9ModuleifMode                 DisplayString   		
    }         

slot9ModuleifIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface.  It
            is recommended that values are assigned contiguously
            starting from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer
            must remain constant at least from one re-initialization of
            the entity's network management system to the next re-
            initialization."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 1 }
    
slot9ModuleIfId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 2 }
    
slot9ModuleifDescr OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A textual string containing information about the
            interface.  This string should include the name of the
            manufacturer, the product name and the version of the
            interface hardware/software."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 3 }
    
slot9ModuleifType OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      IANAifType
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot9ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot9ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot9ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot9ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot9ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot9ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 10 }

slot9ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 11 }

slot9ModuleifInUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were not addressed to a multicast
            or broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 12 }

slot9ModuleifInNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were addressed to a multicast or
            broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifInMulticastPkts and
            ifInBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 13 }

slot9ModuleifInDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of inbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent

            their being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  One
            possible reason for discarding such a packet could be to
            free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 14 }

slot9ModuleifInErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of inbound
            packets that contained errors preventing them from being
            deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  For character-
            oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the number of inbound
            transmission units that contained errors preventing them
            from being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 15 }

slot9ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 16 }

slot9ModuleifInUnknownProtos OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of packets
            received via the interface which were discarded because of
            an unknown or unsupported protocol.  For character-oriented
            or fixed-length interfaces that support protocol
            multiplexing the number of transmission units received via
            the interface which were discarded because of an unknown or
            unsupported protocol.  For any interface that does not
            support protocol multiplexing, this counter will always be
            0.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 17 }

slot9ModuleifOutOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets transmitted out of the
            interface, including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 18 }

slot9ModuleifOutUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were not addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at

            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 19 }

slot9ModuleifOutNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE

    MAX-ACCESS  read-only

slot9ModuleifSpecific OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      OBJECT IDENTIFIER
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "A reference to MIB definitions specific to the particular
            media being used to realize the interface.  It is

            recommended that this value point to an instance of a MIB
            object in the media-specific MIB, i.e., that this object
            have the semantics associated with the InstancePointer
            textual convention defined in RFC 2579.  In fact, it is
            recommended that the media-specific MIB specify what value
            ifSpecific should/can take for values of ifType.  If no MIB
            definitions specific to the particular media are available,
            the value should be set to the OBJECT IDENTIFIER { 0 0 }."
    ::= { slot9ModuleIfEntry 31 }

    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))

-- slot 10 --

-- slot10Table --

slot10Table OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot10Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot10Type's utilization."
    ::= { slot10 1 }  

slot10Entry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot10Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot10's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot10Index }
    ::= { slot10Table 1 }

Slot10Entry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot10Index                       Integer32,
		slot10Type                        DisplayString,
		slot10Status                      DisplayString,		
        slot10SerialNumber                DisplayString,		
        slot10Temperature                 DisplayString
    }  

slot10Index OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot10."
    ::= { slot10Entry 1 }

slot10Type OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the slot10Type of each chassis."
    ::= { slot10Entry 2 }

slot10Status OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board status." 
   ::= { slot10Entry 3 }   
 
slot10SerialNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board serial number." 
    ::= { slot10Entry 4 }   

slot10Temperature OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board temperature." 
    ::= { slot10Entry 5 }   

slot10Module OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { slot10 2 }

-- slot10ModuleTable --
slot10ModuleTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot10ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot10Module's utilization."
    ::= { slot10Module 1 }  

slot10ModuleEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot10ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot10Module's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot10ModuleIndex }
    ::= { slot10ModuleTable 1 }

Slot10ModuleEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot10ModuleIndex                       Integer32,
		slot10ModuleId                           DisplayString,  
		slot10ModuleIfNumber                     Integer32		
    } 

slot10ModuleIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot10."
    ::= { slot10ModuleEntry 1 }

slot10ModuleId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot10ModuleEntry 2 }
  
slot10ModuleIfNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(0..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of network interfaces (regardless of their
            current state) present on this system." 
    ::= { slot10ModuleEntry 3 } 
    
slot10ModuleIfTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot10ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of interface entries.  The number of entries is
            given by the value of ifNumber."
    ::= { slot10Module 2 } 
    
slot10ModuleIfEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot10ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry containing management information applicable to a
            particular interface."
    INDEX   { slot10ModuleifIndex }
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfTable 1 }
    
Slot10ModuleIfEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {
        slot10ModuleifIndex                 InterfaceIndex,  
        slot10ModuleIfId                    DisplayString,  
        slot10ModuleifDescr                 DisplayString,           
        slot10ModuleifType                  IANAifType,   		
        slot10ModuleifMtu                   Integer32,                
        slot10ModuleifSpeed                 Counter64,               
        slot10ModuleifPhysAddress           PhysAddress,              
        slot10ModuleifAdminStatus           INTEGER,                  
        slot10ModuleifOperStatus            INTEGER,                  
        slot10ModuleifLastChange            TimeTicks,                
        slot10ModuleifInOctets              Counter64,                
        slot10ModuleifInUcastPkts           Counter64,                
        slot10ModuleifInNUcastPkts          Counter64,  
        slot10ModuleifInDiscards            Counter64,
        slot10ModuleifInErrors              Counter64,
        slot10ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts        Counter64,
        slot10ModuleifInUnknownProtos       Counter64,	-- deprecated
        slot10ModuleifOutOctets             Counter64,
        slot10ModuleifOutUcastPkts          Counter64,
        slot10ModuleifOutNUcastPkts         Counter64,  -- deprecated
        slot10ModuleifOutDiscards           Counter64,
        slot10ModuleifOutErrors             Counter64,
        slot10ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts       Counter64,
        slot10ModuleifOutQLen               Gauge32,    -- deprecated  
        slot10ModuleifOutOctetsRate         Counter64,
        slot10ModuleifInOctetsRate          Counter64,
        slot10ModuleifOutPktsRate           Counter64,
        slot10ModuleifInPktsRate            Counter64,
        slot10ModuleifRxPower               DisplayString,
        slot10ModuleifTxPower               DisplayString,
        slot10ModuleifSpecific              OBJECT IDENTIFIER,
        slot10ModuleifTxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot10ModuleifRxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot10ModuleifRxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot10ModuleifRxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot10ModuleifTxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot10ModuleifTxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot10ModuleifRxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot10ModuleifTxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot10ModuleifMode                 DisplayString   		
    }         

slot10ModuleifIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface.  It
            is recommended that values are assigned contiguously
            starting from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer
            must remain constant at least from one re-initialization of
            the entity's network management system to the next re-
            initialization."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 1 }
    
slot10ModuleIfId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 2 }
    
slot10ModuleifDescr OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A textual string containing information about the
            interface.  This string should include the name of the
            manufacturer, the product name and the version of the
            interface hardware/software."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 3 }
    
slot10ModuleifType OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      IANAifType
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot10ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot10ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot10ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot10ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot10ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot10ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 10 }

slot10ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 11 }

slot10ModuleifInUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were not addressed to a multicast
            or broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 12 }

slot10ModuleifInNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were addressed to a multicast or
            broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifInMulticastPkts and
            ifInBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 13 }

slot10ModuleifInDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of inbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent

            their being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  One
            possible reason for discarding such a packet could be to
            free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 14 }

slot10ModuleifInErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of inbound
            packets that contained errors preventing them from being
            deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  For character-
            oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the number of inbound
            transmission units that contained errors preventing them
            from being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 15 }

slot10ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 16 }

slot10ModuleifInUnknownProtos OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of packets
            received via the interface which were discarded because of
            an unknown or unsupported protocol.  For character-oriented
            or fixed-length interfaces that support protocol
            multiplexing the number of transmission units received via
            the interface which were discarded because of an unknown or
            unsupported protocol.  For any interface that does not
            support protocol multiplexing, this counter will always be
            0.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 17 }

slot10ModuleifOutOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets transmitted out of the
            interface, including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 18 }

slot10ModuleifOutUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were not addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 19 }

slot10ModuleifOutNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifOutMulticastPkts
            and ifOutBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 20 }

slot10ModuleifOutDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of outbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent
            their being transmitted.  One possible reason for discarding
            such a packet could be to free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 21 }

slot10ModuleifOutErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of outbound
            packets that could not be transmitted because of errors.
            For character-oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the
            number of outbound transmission units that could not be
            transmitted because of errors.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 22 }

slot10ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 23 }

slot10ModuleifOutQLen OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Gauge32
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The length of the output packet queue (in packets)."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 24 }

slot10ModuleifOutOctetsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets trans on the interface(kbps)"

    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "A reference to MIB definitions specific to the particular
            media being used to realize the interface.  It is

            recommended that this value point to an instance of a MIB
            object in the media-specific MIB, i.e., that this object
            have the semantics associated with the InstancePointer
            textual convention defined in RFC 2579.  In fact, it is
            recommended that the media-specific MIB specify what value
            ifSpecific should/can take for values of ifType.  If no MIB
            definitions specific to the particular media are available,
            the value should be set to the OBJECT IDENTIFIER { 0 0 }."
    ::= { slot10ModuleIfEntry 31 }

            "An entry contains a slot11's utilization."

    SEQUENCE {     
		slot11Index                       Integer32,
		slot11Type                        DisplayString,

    }

    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)

    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current

            "A string to describe the board serial number."

slot11Temperature OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only

    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board temperature." 
    ::= { slot11Entry 5 }   


slot11Module OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { slot11 2 }

-- slot11ModuleTable --
slot11ModuleTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot11ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot11Module's utilization."
    ::= { slot11Module 1 }  

slot11ModuleEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot11ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot11Module's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot11ModuleIndex }
    ::= { slot11ModuleTable 1 }

Slot11ModuleEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot11ModuleIndex                       Integer32,
		slot11ModuleId                           DisplayString,  
		slot11ModuleIfNumber                     Integer32		
    } 

slot11ModuleIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot11."
    ::= { slot11ModuleEntry 1 }

slot11ModuleId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot11ModuleEntry 2 }
  
slot11ModuleIfNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(0..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of network interfaces (regardless of their
            current state) present on this system." 
    ::= { slot11ModuleEntry 3 } 
    
slot11ModuleIfTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot11ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of interface entries.  The number of entries is
            given by the value of ifNumber."
    ::= { slot11Module 2 } 
    
slot11ModuleIfEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot11ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry containing management information applicable to a
            particular interface."
    INDEX   { slot11ModuleifIndex }
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfTable 1 }
    
Slot11ModuleIfEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {
        slot11ModuleifIndex                 InterfaceIndex,  
        slot11ModuleIfId                    DisplayString,  
        slot11ModuleifDescr                 DisplayString,           
        slot11ModuleifType                  IANAifType,   		
        slot11ModuleifMtu                   Integer32,                
        slot11ModuleifSpeed                 Counter64,               
        slot11ModuleifPhysAddress           PhysAddress,              
        slot11ModuleifAdminStatus           INTEGER,                  
        slot11ModuleifOperStatus            INTEGER,                  
        slot11ModuleifLastChange            TimeTicks,                
        slot11ModuleifInOctets              Counter64,                
        slot11ModuleifInUcastPkts           Counter64,                
        slot11ModuleifInNUcastPkts          Counter64,  
        slot11ModuleifInDiscards            Counter64,
        slot11ModuleifInErrors              Counter64,
        slot11ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts        Counter64,
        slot11ModuleifInUnknownProtos       Counter64,	-- deprecated
        slot11ModuleifOutOctets             Counter64,
        slot11ModuleifOutUcastPkts          Counter64,
        slot11ModuleifOutNUcastPkts         Counter64,  -- deprecated
        slot11ModuleifOutDiscards           Counter64,
        slot11ModuleifOutErrors             Counter64,
        slot11ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts       Counter64,
        slot11ModuleifOutQLen               Gauge32,    -- deprecated  
        slot11ModuleifOutOctetsRate         Counter64,
        slot11ModuleifInOctetsRate          Counter64,
        slot11ModuleifOutPktsRate           Counter64,
        slot11ModuleifInPktsRate            Counter64,
        slot11ModuleifRxPower               DisplayString,
        slot11ModuleifTxPower               DisplayString,
        slot11ModuleifSpecific              OBJECT IDENTIFIER,
        slot11ModuleifTxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot11ModuleifRxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot11ModuleifRxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot11ModuleifRxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot11ModuleifTxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot11ModuleifTxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot11ModuleifRxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot11ModuleifTxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot11ModuleifMode                 DisplayString   		
    }         

slot11ModuleifIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface.  It
            is recommended that values are assigned contiguously
            starting from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer
            must remain constant at least from one re-initialization of
            the entity's network management system to the next re-
            initialization."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 1 }
    
slot11ModuleIfId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 2 }
    
slot11ModuleifDescr OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A textual string containing information about the
            interface.  This string should include the name of the
            manufacturer, the product name and the version of the
            interface hardware/software."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 3 }
    
slot11ModuleifType OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      IANAifType
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot11ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot11ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot11ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot11ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot11ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot11ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 10 }


slot11ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 11 }

slot11ModuleifInUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were not addressed to a multicast
            or broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 12 }

slot11ModuleifInNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were addressed to a multicast or
            broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifInMulticastPkts and
            ifInBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 13 }

slot11ModuleifInDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of inbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent

            their being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  One
            possible reason for discarding such a packet could be to
            free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 14 }

slot11ModuleifInErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of inbound
            packets that contained errors preventing them from being
            deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  For character-
            oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the number of inbound
            transmission units that contained errors preventing them
            from being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 15 }

slot11ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 16 }

slot11ModuleifInUnknownProtos OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of packets
            received via the interface which were discarded because of
            an unknown or unsupported protocol.  For character-oriented
            or fixed-length interfaces that support protocol
            multiplexing the number of transmission units received via
            the interface which were discarded because of an unknown or
            unsupported protocol.  For any interface that does not
            support protocol multiplexing, this counter will always be
            0.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 17 }

slot11ModuleifOutOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets transmitted out of the
            interface, including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 18 }

slot11ModuleifOutUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were not addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 19 }

slot11ModuleifOutNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifOutMulticastPkts
            and ifOutBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 20 }

slot11ModuleifOutDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of outbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent
            their being transmitted.  One possible reason for discarding
            such a packet could be to free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 21 }

slot11ModuleifOutErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of outbound
            packets that could not be transmitted because of errors.
            For character-oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the
            number of outbound transmission units that could not be
            transmitted because of errors.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 22 }

slot11ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 23 }

slot11ModuleifOutQLen OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Gauge32
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The length of the output packet queue (in packets)."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 24 }

slot11ModuleifOutOctetsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets trans on the interface(kbps)"
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 25 }

            "The speed of packets trans on the interface(pps)"
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 27 }

slot11ModuleifSpecific OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      OBJECT IDENTIFIER
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "A reference to MIB definitions specific to the particular
            media being used to realize the interface.  It is

            recommended that this value point to an instance of a MIB
            object in the media-specific MIB, i.e., that this object
            have the semantics associated with the InstancePointer
            textual convention defined in RFC 2579.  In fact, it is
            recommended that the media-specific MIB specify what value
            ifSpecific should/can take for values of ifType.  If no MIB
            definitions specific to the particular media are available,
            the value should be set to the OBJECT IDENTIFIER { 0 0 }."
    ::= { slot11ModuleIfEntry 31 }

slot12ModuleifIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface.  It
            is recommended that values are assigned contiguously
            starting from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer
            must remain constant at least from one re-initialization of
            the entity's network management system to the next re-
            initialization."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 1 }
    
slot12ModuleIfId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 2 }
    
slot12ModuleifDescr OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A textual string containing information about the
            interface.  This string should include the name of the
            manufacturer, the product name and the version of the
            interface hardware/software."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 3 }
    
slot12ModuleifType OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      IANAifType
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot12ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot12ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot12ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot12ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot12ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot12ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 10 }

slot12ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 11 }

slot12ModuleifInUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were not addressed to a multicast
            or broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 12 }

slot12ModuleifInNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were addressed to a multicast or
            broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifInMulticastPkts and
            ifInBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 13 }

slot12ModuleifInDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of inbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent

            their being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  One
            possible reason for discarding such a packet could be to
            free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 14 }

slot12ModuleifInErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of inbound
            packets that contained errors preventing them from being
            deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  For character-
            oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the number of inbound
            transmission units that contained errors preventing them
            from being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 15 }

slot12ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 16 }

slot12ModuleifInUnknownProtos OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of packets
            received via the interface which were discarded because of
            an unknown or unsupported protocol.  For character-oriented
            or fixed-length interfaces that support protocol
            multiplexing the number of transmission units received via
            the interface which were discarded because of an unknown or
            unsupported protocol.  For any interface that does not
            support protocol multiplexing, this counter will always be
            0.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 17 }

slot12ModuleifOutOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets transmitted out of the
            interface, including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 18 }

slot12ModuleifOutUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were not addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 19 }

slot12ModuleifOutNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifOutMulticastPkts
            and ifOutBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 20 }

slot12ModuleifOutDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of outbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent
            their being transmitted.  One possible reason for discarding
            such a packet could be to free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 21 }

slot12ModuleifOutErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of outbound
            packets that could not be transmitted because of errors.
            For character-oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the
            number of outbound transmission units that could not be
            transmitted because of errors.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 22 }

slot12ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 23 }

slot12ModuleifOutQLen OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Gauge32
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The length of the output packet queue (in packets)."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 24 }

slot12ModuleifOutOctetsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets trans on the interface(kbps)"
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 25 }

slot12ModuleifInOctetsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets received on the interface(kbps)"
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 26 }

slot12ModuleifOutPktsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of packets trans on the interface(pps)"
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 27 }

slot12ModuleifInPktsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets received on the interface(kbps)"
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 28 }

slot12ModuleifRxPower OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of interface's received power, in dbm format."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 29 }

slot12ModuleifTxPower OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of interface's send power, in dbm format."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 30 }

slot12ModuleifSpecific OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      OBJECT IDENTIFIER
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "A reference to MIB definitions specific to the particular
            media being used to realize the interface.  It is

            recommended that this value point to an instance of a MIB
            object in the media-specific MIB, i.e., that this object
            have the semantics associated with the InstancePointer
            textual convention defined in RFC 2579.  In fact, it is
            recommended that the media-specific MIB specify what value
            ifSpecific should/can take for values of ifType.  If no MIB
            definitions specific to the particular media are available,
            the value should be set to the OBJECT IDENTIFIER { 0 0 }."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 31 }  
   
slot12ModuleifTxMirrorList OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "the interface tx mirror list."
    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 32 }

    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))

    ::= { slot12ModuleIfEntry 35 }

    DESCRIPTION
