-- slot 13 --

-- slot13Table --

slot13Table OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot13Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot13Type's utilization."
    ::= { slot13 1 }  

slot13Entry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot13Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot13's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot13Index }
    ::= { slot13Table 1 }

Slot13Entry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot13Index                       Integer32,
		slot13Type                        DisplayString,
		slot13Status                      DisplayString,		
        slot13SerialNumber                DisplayString,		
        slot13Temperature                 DisplayString
    }  

slot13Index OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot13."
    ::= { slot13Entry 1 }

slot13Type OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the slot13Type of each chassis."
    ::= { slot13Entry 2 }

slot13Status OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board status." 
    ::= { slot13Entry 3 }   

slot13SerialNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board serial number." 
    ::= { slot13Entry 4 }   

slot13Temperature OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board temperature." 
    ::= { slot13Entry 5 }   


slot13Module OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { slot13 2 }

-- slot13ModuleTable --
slot13ModuleTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot13ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot13Module's utilization."
    ::= { slot13Module 1 }  

slot13ModuleEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot13ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot13Module's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot13ModuleIndex }
    ::= { slot13ModuleTable 1 }

Slot13ModuleEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot13ModuleIndex                       Integer32,
		slot13ModuleId                           DisplayString,  
		slot13ModuleIfNumber                     Integer32		
    } 

slot13ModuleIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot13."
    ::= { slot13ModuleEntry 1 }

slot13ModuleId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot13ModuleEntry 2 }
  
slot13ModuleIfNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(0..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of network interfaces (regardless of their
            current state) present on this system." 
    ::= { slot13ModuleEntry 3 } 
    
slot13ModuleIfTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot13ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of interface entries.  The number of entries is
            given by the value of ifNumber."
    ::= { slot13Module 2 } 
    
slot13ModuleIfEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot13ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry containing management information applicable to a
            particular interface."
    INDEX   { slot13ModuleifIndex }
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfTable 1 }
    
Slot13ModuleIfEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {
        slot13ModuleifIndex                 InterfaceIndex,  
        slot13ModuleIfId                    DisplayString,  
        slot13ModuleifDescr                 DisplayString,           
        slot13ModuleifType                  IANAifType,   		
        slot13ModuleifMtu                   Integer32,                
        slot13ModuleifSpeed                 Counter64,               
        slot13ModuleifPhysAddress           PhysAddress,              
        slot13ModuleifAdminStatus           INTEGER,                  
        slot13ModuleifOperStatus            INTEGER,                  
        slot13ModuleifLastChange            TimeTicks,                
        slot13ModuleifInOctets              Counter64,                
        slot13ModuleifInUcastPkts           Counter64,                
        slot13ModuleifInNUcastPkts          Counter64, 
        slot13ModuleifInDiscards            Counter64,
        slot13ModuleifInErrors              Counter64,
        slot13ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts        Counter64,
        slot13ModuleifInUnknownProtos       Counter64,	-- deprecated
        slot13ModuleifOutOctets             Counter64,
        slot13ModuleifOutUcastPkts          Counter64,
        slot13ModuleifOutNUcastPkts         Counter64,  -- deprecated
        slot13ModuleifOutDiscards           Counter64,
        slot13ModuleifOutErrors             Counter64,
        slot13ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts       Counter64,
        slot13ModuleifOutQLen               Gauge32,    -- deprecated  
        slot13ModuleifOutOctetsRate         Counter64,
        slot13ModuleifInOctetsRate          Counter64,
        slot13ModuleifOutPktsRate           Counter64,
        slot13ModuleifInPktsRate            Counter64,
        slot13ModuleifRxPower               DisplayString,
        slot13ModuleifTxPower               DisplayString,
        slot13ModuleifSpecific              OBJECT IDENTIFIER,
        slot13ModuleifTxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot13ModuleifRxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot13ModuleifRxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot13ModuleifRxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot13ModuleifTxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot13ModuleifTxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot13ModuleifRxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot13ModuleifTxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot13ModuleifMode                 DisplayString   		
    }         

slot13ModuleifIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface.  It
            is recommended that values are assigned contiguously
            starting from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer
            must remain constant at least from one re-initialization of
            the entity's network management system to the next re-
            initialization."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 1 }
    
slot13ModuleIfId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 2 }
    
slot13ModuleifDescr OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A textual string containing information about the
            interface.  This string should include the name of the
            manufacturer, the product name and the version of the
            interface hardware/software."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 3 }
    
slot13ModuleifType OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      IANAifType
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot13ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot13ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot13ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot13ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot13ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot13ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 10 }


slot13ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 11 }

slot13ModuleifInUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were not addressed to a multicast
            or broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 12 }

slot13ModuleifInNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were addressed to a multicast or
            broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifInMulticastPkts and
            ifInBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 13 }

slot13ModuleifInDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of inbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent

            their being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  One
            possible reason for discarding such a packet could be to
            free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 14 }

slot13ModuleifInErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of inbound
            packets that contained errors preventing them from being
            deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  For character-
            oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the number of inbound
            transmission units that contained errors preventing them
            from being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 15 }

slot13ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 16 }

slot13ModuleifInUnknownProtos OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of packets
            received via the interface which were discarded because of
            an unknown or unsupported protocol.  For character-oriented
            or fixed-length interfaces that support protocol
            multiplexing the number of transmission units received via
            the interface which were discarded because of an unknown or
            unsupported protocol.  For any interface that does not
            support protocol multiplexing, this counter will always be
            0.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 17 }

slot13ModuleifOutOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets transmitted out of the
            interface, including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 18 }

slot13ModuleifOutUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were not addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 19 }

slot13ModuleifOutNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifOutMulticastPkts
            and ifOutBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 20 }

slot13ModuleifOutDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of outbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent
            their being transmitted.  One possible reason for discarding
            such a packet could be to free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 21 }

slot13ModuleifOutErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of outbound
            packets that could not be transmitted because of errors.
            For character-oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the
            number of outbound transmission units that could not be
            transmitted because of errors.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 22 }

slot13ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 23 }

slot13ModuleifOutQLen OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Gauge32
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The length of the output packet queue (in packets)."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 24 }

slot13ModuleifOutOctetsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets trans on the interface(kbps)"

slot13ModuleifSpecific OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      OBJECT IDENTIFIER
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "A reference to MIB definitions specific to the particular
            media being used to realize the interface.  It is

            recommended that this value point to an instance of a MIB
            object in the media-specific MIB, i.e., that this object
            have the semantics associated with the InstancePointer
            textual convention defined in RFC 2579.  In fact, it is
            recommended that the media-specific MIB specify what value
            ifSpecific should/can take for values of ifType.  If no MIB
            definitions specific to the particular media are available,
            the value should be set to the OBJECT IDENTIFIER { 0 0 }."
    ::= { slot13ModuleIfEntry 31 }

-- slot 14 --

-- slot14Table --

slot14Table OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot14Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot14Type's utilization."
    ::= { slot14 1 }  

slot14Entry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot14Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot14's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot14Index }
    ::= { slot14Table 1 }

Slot14Entry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot14Index                       Integer32,
		slot14Type                        DisplayString,
		slot14Status                      DisplayString,
        slot14SerialNumber                DisplayString,		
        slot14Temperature                 DisplayString
    }  

slot14Index OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot14."
    ::= { slot14Entry 1 }

slot14Type OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the slot14Type of each chassis."
    ::= { slot14Entry 2 }

slot14Status OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board status." 
    ::= { slot14Entry 3 }   

slot14SerialNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board serial number." 
    ::= { slot14Entry 4 }   

slot14Temperature OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board temperature." 
    ::= { slot14Entry 5 }   


slot14Module OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { slot14 2 }

-- slot14ModuleTable --
slot14ModuleTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot14ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot14Module's utilization."
    ::= { slot14Module 1 }  

slot14ModuleEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot14ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot14Module's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot14ModuleIndex }
    ::= { slot14ModuleTable 1 }

Slot14ModuleEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot14ModuleIndex                       Integer32,
		slot14ModuleId                           DisplayString,  
		slot14ModuleIfNumber                     Integer32		
    } 

slot14ModuleIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot14."
    ::= { slot14ModuleEntry 1 }

slot14ModuleId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot14ModuleEntry 2 }
  
slot14ModuleIfNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(0..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of network interfaces (regardless of their
            current state) present on this system." 
    ::= { slot14ModuleEntry 3 } 
    
slot14ModuleIfTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot14ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of interface entries.  The number of entries is
            given by the value of ifNumber."
    ::= { slot14Module 2 } 
    
slot14ModuleIfEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot14ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry containing management information applicable to a
            particular interface."
    INDEX   { slot14ModuleifIndex }
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfTable 1 }
    
Slot14ModuleIfEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {
        slot14ModuleifIndex                 InterfaceIndex,  
        slot14ModuleIfId                    DisplayString,  
        slot14ModuleifDescr                 DisplayString,           
        slot14ModuleifType                  IANAifType,   		
        slot14ModuleifMtu                   Integer32,                
        slot14ModuleifSpeed                 Counter64,               
        slot14ModuleifPhysAddress           PhysAddress,              
        slot14ModuleifAdminStatus           INTEGER,                  
        slot14ModuleifOperStatus            INTEGER,                  
        slot14ModuleifLastChange            TimeTicks,                
        slot14ModuleifInOctets              Counter64,                
        slot14ModuleifInUcastPkts           Counter64,                
        slot14ModuleifInNUcastPkts          Counter64,  
        slot14ModuleifInDiscards            Counter64,
        slot14ModuleifInErrors              Counter64,
        slot14ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts        Counter64,
        slot14ModuleifInUnknownProtos       Counter64,	-- deprecated
        slot14ModuleifOutOctets             Counter64,
        slot14ModuleifOutUcastPkts          Counter64,
        slot14ModuleifOutNUcastPkts         Counter64,  -- deprecated
        slot14ModuleifOutDiscards           Counter64,
        slot14ModuleifOutErrors             Counter64,
        slot14ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts       Counter64,
        slot14ModuleifOutQLen               Gauge32,    -- deprecated  
        slot14ModuleifOutOctetsRate         Counter64,
        slot14ModuleifInOctetsRate          Counter64,
        slot14ModuleifOutPktsRate           Counter64,
        slot14ModuleifInPktsRate            Counter64,
        slot14ModuleifRxPower               DisplayString,
        slot14ModuleifTxPower               DisplayString,
        slot14ModuleifSpecific              OBJECT IDENTIFIER,
        slot14ModuleifTxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot14ModuleifRxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot14ModuleifRxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot14ModuleifRxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot14ModuleifTxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot14ModuleifTxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot14ModuleifRxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot14ModuleifTxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot14ModuleifMode                 DisplayString   		
    }         

slot14ModuleifIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface.  It
            is recommended that values are assigned contiguously
            starting from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer
            must remain constant at least from one re-initialization of
            the entity's network management system to the next re-
            initialization."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 1 }
    
slot14ModuleIfId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 2 }
    
slot14ModuleifDescr OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A textual string containing information about the
            interface.  This string should include the name of the
            manufacturer, the product name and the version of the
            interface hardware/software."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 3 }
    
slot14ModuleifType OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      IANAifType
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot14ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot14ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot14ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot14ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot14ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot14ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 10 }

slot14ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 11 }

slot14ModuleifInUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other

            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 12 }

    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 13 }

slot14ModuleifInDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of inbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent

            their being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  One
            possible reason for discarding such a packet could be to
            free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 14 }

slot14ModuleifInErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of inbound
            packets that contained errors preventing them from being
            deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  For character-
            oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the number of inbound
            transmission units that contained errors preventing them
            from being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 15 }

slot14ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 16 }

slot14ModuleifInUnknownProtos OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of packets
            received via the interface which were discarded because of
            an unknown or unsupported protocol.  For character-oriented
            or fixed-length interfaces that support protocol
            multiplexing the number of transmission units received via
            the interface which were discarded because of an unknown or
            unsupported protocol.  For any interface that does not
            support protocol multiplexing, this counter will always be
            0.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 17 }

slot14ModuleifOutOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets transmitted out of the
            interface, including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 18 }

slot14ModuleifOutUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were not addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 19 }

slot14ModuleifOutNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifOutMulticastPkts
            and ifOutBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 20 }

slot14ModuleifOutDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of outbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent
            their being transmitted.  One possible reason for discarding
            such a packet could be to free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 21 }

slot14ModuleifOutErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of outbound
            packets that could not be transmitted because of errors.
            For character-oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the
            number of outbound transmission units that could not be
            transmitted because of errors.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 22 }

slot14ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 23 }

    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The length of the output packet queue (in packets)."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 24 }

slot14ModuleifSpecific OBJECT-TYPE

    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "A reference to MIB definitions specific to the particular
            media being used to realize the interface.  It is

            recommended that this value point to an instance of a MIB
            object in the media-specific MIB, i.e., that this object
            have the semantics associated with the InstancePointer
            textual convention defined in RFC 2579.  In fact, it is
            recommended that the media-specific MIB specify what value
            ifSpecific should/can take for values of ifType.  If no MIB
            definitions specific to the particular media are available,
            the value should be set to the OBJECT IDENTIFIER { 0 0 }."
    ::= { slot14ModuleIfEntry 31 }

-- slot 15 --

-- slot15Table --

slot15Table OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot15Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot15Type's utilization."
    ::= { slot15 1 }  

slot15Entry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot15Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot15's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot15Index }
    ::= { slot15Table 1 }

Slot15Entry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot15Index                       Integer32,
		slot15Type                        DisplayString,
		slot15Status                      DisplayString,
        slot15SerialNumber                DisplayString,		
        slot15Temperature                 DisplayString
    }  

slot15Index OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot15."
    ::= { slot15Entry 1 }

slot15Type OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the slot15Type of each chassis."
    ::= { slot15Entry 2 }

slot15Status OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board status." 
    ::= { slot15Entry 3 }   

slot15SerialNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board serial number." 
    ::= { slot15Entry 4 }   

slot15Temperature OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board temperature." 
    ::= { slot15Entry 5 }   


slot15Module OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { slot15 2 }

-- slot15ModuleTable --
slot15ModuleTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot15ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot15Module's utilization."
    ::= { slot15Module 1 }  

slot15ModuleEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot15ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot15Module's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot15ModuleIndex }
    ::= { slot15ModuleTable 1 }

Slot15ModuleEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot15ModuleIndex                       Integer32,
		slot15ModuleId                           DisplayString,  
		slot15ModuleIfNumber                     Integer32		
    } 

slot15ModuleIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot15."
    ::= { slot15ModuleEntry 1 }

slot15ModuleId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot15ModuleEntry 2 }
  
slot15ModuleIfNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(0..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of network interfaces (regardless of their
            current state) present on this system." 
    ::= { slot15ModuleEntry 3 } 
    
slot15ModuleIfTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot15ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of interface entries.  The number of entries is
            given by the value of ifNumber."
    ::= { slot15Module 2 } 
    
slot15ModuleIfEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot15ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry containing management information applicable to a
            particular interface."
    INDEX   { slot15ModuleifIndex }
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfTable 1 }
    
Slot15ModuleIfEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {
        slot15ModuleifIndex                 InterfaceIndex,  
        slot15ModuleIfId                    DisplayString,  
        slot15ModuleifDescr                 DisplayString,           
        slot15ModuleifType                  IANAifType,   		
        slot15ModuleifMtu                   Integer32,                
        slot15ModuleifSpeed                 Counter64,               
        slot15ModuleifPhysAddress           PhysAddress,              
        slot15ModuleifAdminStatus           INTEGER,                  
        slot15ModuleifOperStatus            INTEGER,                  
        slot15ModuleifLastChange            TimeTicks,                
        slot15ModuleifInOctets              Counter64,                
        slot15ModuleifInUcastPkts           Counter64,                
        slot15ModuleifInNUcastPkts          Counter64,  
        slot15ModuleifInDiscards            Counter64,
        slot15ModuleifInErrors              Counter64,
        slot15ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts        Counter64,
        slot15ModuleifInUnknownProtos       Counter64,	-- deprecated
        slot15ModuleifOutOctets             Counter64,
        slot15ModuleifOutUcastPkts          Counter64,
        slot15ModuleifOutNUcastPkts         Counter64,  -- deprecated
        slot15ModuleifOutDiscards           Counter64,
        slot15ModuleifOutErrors             Counter64,
        slot15ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts       Counter64,
        slot15ModuleifOutQLen               Gauge32,    -- deprecated  
        slot15ModuleifOutOctetsRate         Counter64,
        slot15ModuleifInOctetsRate          Counter64,
        slot15ModuleifOutPktsRate           Counter64,
        slot15ModuleifInPktsRate            Counter64,
        slot15ModuleifRxPower               DisplayString,
        slot15ModuleifTxPower               DisplayString,
        slot15ModuleifSpecific              OBJECT IDENTIFIER,
        slot15ModuleifTxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot15ModuleifRxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot15ModuleifRxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot15ModuleifRxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot15ModuleifTxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot15ModuleifTxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot15ModuleifRxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot15ModuleifTxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot15ModuleifMode                 DisplayString   		
    }         

slot15ModuleifIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface.  It
            is recommended that values are assigned contiguously
            starting from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer
            must remain constant at least from one re-initialization of
            the entity's network management system to the next re-
            initialization."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 1 }
    
slot15ModuleIfId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 2 }
    
slot15ModuleifDescr OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A textual string containing information about the
            interface.  This string should include the name of the
            manufacturer, the product name and the version of the
            interface hardware/software."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 3 }
    
slot15ModuleifType OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      IANAifType
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot15ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot15ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot15ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot15ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot15ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot15ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 10 }

slot15ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 11 }

slot15ModuleifInUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were not addressed to a multicast
            or broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 12 }

slot15ModuleifInNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were addressed to a multicast or
            broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifInMulticastPkts and
            ifInBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 13 }

slot15ModuleifInDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of inbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent

            their being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  One
            possible reason for discarding such a packet could be to
            free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 14 }

slot15ModuleifInErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of inbound
            packets that contained errors preventing them from being
            deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  For character-
            oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the number of inbound
            transmission units that contained errors preventing them
            from being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 15 }

slot15ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 16 }

slot15ModuleifInUnknownProtos OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of packets
            received via the interface which were discarded because of
            an unknown or unsupported protocol.  For character-oriented
            or fixed-length interfaces that support protocol
            multiplexing the number of transmission units received via
            the interface which were discarded because of an unknown or
            unsupported protocol.  For any interface that does not
            support protocol multiplexing, this counter will always be
            0.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 17 }

slot15ModuleifOutOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets transmitted out of the
            interface, including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 18 }

slot15ModuleifOutUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were not addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 19 }

slot15ModuleifOutNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were addressed to a

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at

    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 20 }

    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 21 }

slot15ModuleifOutErrors OBJECT-TYPE

    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 27 }

slot15ModuleifInPktsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets received on the interface(kbps)"
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 28 }

slot15ModuleifRxPower OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of interface's received power, in dbm format."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 29 }

slot15ModuleifTxPower OBJECT-TYPE

    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION

    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 30 }

slot15ModuleifSpecific OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      OBJECT IDENTIFIER
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "A reference to MIB definitions specific to the particular
            media being used to realize the interface.  It is

            recommended that this value point to an instance of a MIB
            object in the media-specific MIB, i.e., that this object
            have the semantics associated with the InstancePointer
            textual convention defined in RFC 2579.  In fact, it is
            recommended that the media-specific MIB specify what value
            ifSpecific should/can take for values of ifType.  If no MIB
            definitions specific to the particular media are available,
            the value should be set to the OBJECT IDENTIFIER { 0 0 }."
    ::= { slot15ModuleIfEntry 31 }
