-- slot 16 --

-- slot16Table --

slot16Table OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot16Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot16Type's utilization."
    ::= { slot16 1 }  

slot16Entry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot16Entry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot16's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot16Index }
    ::= { slot16Table 1 }

Slot16Entry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot16Index                       Integer32,
		slot16Type                        DisplayString,
		slot16Status                      DisplayString,
        slot16SerialNumber                DisplayString,		
        slot16Temperature                 DisplayString
    }  

slot16Index OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot16."
    ::= { slot16Entry 1 }

slot16Type OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the slot16Type of each chassis."
    ::= { slot16Entry 2 }

slot16Status OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board status." 
    ::= { slot16Entry 3 }   

slot16SerialNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board serial number." 
    ::= { slot16Entry 4 }   

slot16Temperature OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A string to describe the board temperature." 
    ::= { slot16Entry 5 }   


slot16Module OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { slot16 2 }

-- slot16ModuleTable --
slot16ModuleTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot16ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of all slot16Module's utilization."
    ::= { slot16Module 1 }  

slot16ModuleEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot16ModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry contains a slot16Module's utilization."
    INDEX   { slot16ModuleIndex }
    ::= { slot16ModuleTable 1 }

Slot16ModuleEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {     
		slot16ModuleIndex                       Integer32,
		slot16ModuleId                           DisplayString,  
		slot16ModuleIfNumber                     Integer32		
    } 

slot16ModuleIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32 (1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each chassis`s slot16."
    ::= { slot16ModuleEntry 1 }

slot16ModuleId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot16ModuleEntry 2 }
  
slot16ModuleIfNumber OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(0..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of network interfaces (regardless of their
            current state) present on this system." 
    ::= { slot16ModuleEntry 3 } 
    
slot16ModuleIfTable OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF Slot16ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A list of interface entries.  The number of entries is
            given by the value of ifNumber."
    ::= { slot16Module 2 } 
    
slot16ModuleIfEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Slot16ModuleIfEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An entry containing management information applicable to a
            particular interface."
    INDEX   { slot16ModuleifIndex }
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfTable 1 }
    
Slot16ModuleIfEntry ::=
    SEQUENCE {
        slot16ModuleifIndex                 InterfaceIndex,  
        slot16ModuleIfId                    DisplayString,  
        slot16ModuleifDescr                 DisplayString,           
        slot16ModuleifType                  IANAifType,   		
        slot16ModuleifMtu                   Integer32,                
        slot16ModuleifSpeed                 Counter64,               
        slot16ModuleifPhysAddress           PhysAddress,              
        slot16ModuleifAdminStatus           INTEGER,                  
        slot16ModuleifOperStatus            INTEGER,                  
        slot16ModuleifLastChange            TimeTicks,                
        slot16ModuleifInOctets              Counter64,                
        slot16ModuleifInUcastPkts           Counter64,                
        slot16ModuleifInNUcastPkts          Counter64,  
        slot16ModuleifInDiscards            Counter64,
        slot16ModuleifInErrors              Counter64,
        slot16ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts        Counter64,
        slot16ModuleifInUnknownProtos       Counter64,	-- deprecated
        slot16ModuleifOutOctets             Counter64,
        slot16ModuleifOutUcastPkts          Counter64,
        slot16ModuleifOutNUcastPkts         Counter64,  -- deprecated
        slot16ModuleifOutDiscards           Counter64,
        slot16ModuleifOutErrors             Counter64,
        slot16ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts       Counter64,
        slot16ModuleifOutQLen               Gauge32,    -- deprecated  
        slot16ModuleifOutOctetsRate         Counter64,
        slot16ModuleifInOctetsRate          Counter64,
        slot16ModuleifOutPktsRate           Counter64,
        slot16ModuleifInPktsRate            Counter64,
        slot16ModuleifRxPower               DisplayString,
        slot16ModuleifTxPower               DisplayString,
        slot16ModuleifSpecific              OBJECT IDENTIFIER,
        slot16ModuleifTxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot16ModuleifRxMirrorList          DisplayString,
        slot16ModuleifRxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot16ModuleifRxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot16ModuleifTxPowerMin               DisplayString,
        slot16ModuleifTxPowerMax               DisplayString,
        slot16ModuleifRxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot16ModuleifTxHisPeak            Counter64,
        slot16ModuleifMode                 DisplayString   		
    }         

slot16ModuleifIndex OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      InterfaceIndex
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A unique value, greater than zero, for each interface.  It
            is recommended that values are assigned contiguously
            starting from 1.  The value for each interface sub-layer
            must remain constant at least from one re-initialization of
            the entity's network management system to the next re-
            initialization."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 1 }
    
slot16ModuleIfId OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..32))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "the value of module`s id"
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 2 }
    
slot16ModuleifDescr OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A textual string containing information about the
            interface.  This string should include the name of the
            manufacturer, the product name and the version of the
            interface hardware/software."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 3 }
    
slot16ModuleifType OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      IANAifType
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The type of interface.  Additional values for ifType are
            assigned by the Internet Assigned Numbers Authority (IANA),
            through updating the syntax of the IANAifType textual
            convention."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 4 }

slot16ModuleifMtu OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Integer32(1..2147483647)
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The size of the largest packet which can be sent/received
            on the interface, specified in octets.  For interfaces that
            are used for transmitting network datagrams, this is the
            size of the largest network datagram that can be sent on the
            interface."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 5 }

slot16ModuleifSpeed OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "An estimate of the interface's current bandwidth in bits
            per second.  For interfaces which do not vary in bandwidth
            or for those where no accurate estimation can be made, this
            object should contain the nominal bandwidth. For a sub-layer
            which has no concept of bandwidth, this object should be zero."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 6 }

slot16ModuleifPhysAddress OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      PhysAddress
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The interface's address at its protocol sub-layer.  For
            example, for an 802.x interface, this object normally
            contains a MAC address.  The interface's media-specific MIB
            must define the bit and byte ordering and the format of the
            value of this object.  For interfaces which do not have such
            an address (e.g., a serial line), this object should contain
            an octet string of zero length."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 7 }
    
slot16ModuleifAdminStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),       -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3)   -- in some test mode
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-write
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The desired state of the interface.  The testing(3) state
            indicates that no operational packets can be passed.  When a
            managed system initializes, all interfaces start with
            ifAdminStatus in the down(2) state.  As a result of either
            explicit management action or per configuration information
            retained by the managed system, ifAdminStatus is then
            changed to either the up(1) or testing(3) states (or remains
            in the down(2) state)."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 8 }

slot16ModuleifOperStatus OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  INTEGER {
                up(1),        -- ready to pass packets
                down(2),
                testing(3),   -- in some test mode
                unknown(4),   -- status can not be determined
                              -- for some reason.
                dormant(5),
                notPresent(6),    -- some component is missing
                lowerLayerDown(7) -- down due to state of
                                  -- lower-layer interface(s)
            }
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The current operational state of the interface.  The
            testing(3) state indicates that no operational packets can
            be passed.  If ifAdminStatus is down(2) then ifOperStatus
            should be down(2).  If ifAdminStatus is changed to up(1)
            then ifOperStatus should change to up(1) if the interface is
            ready to transmit and receive network traffic; it should
            change to dormant(5) if the interface is waiting for
            external actions (such as a serial line waiting for an
            incoming connection); it should remain in the down(2) state
            if and only if there is a fault that prevents it from going
            to the up(1) state; it should remain in the notPresent(6)
            state if the interface has missing (typically, hardware)
            components."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 9 }

slot16ModuleifLastChange OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      TimeTicks
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The value of sysUpTime at the time the interface entered
            its current operational state.  If the current state was
            entered prior to the last re-initialization of the local
            network management subsystem, then this object contains a
            zero value."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 10 }

slot16ModuleifInOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets received on the interface,
            including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 11 }

slot16ModuleifInUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were not addressed to a multicast
            or broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 12 }

slot16ModuleifInNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of packets, delivered by this sub-layer to a
            higher (sub-)layer, which were addressed to a multicast or
            broadcast address at this sub-layer.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifInMulticastPkts and
            ifInBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 13 }

slot16ModuleifInDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of inbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent

            their being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  One
            possible reason for discarding such a packet could be to
            free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 14 }

slot16ModuleifInErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of inbound
            packets that contained errors preventing them from being
            deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.  For character-
            oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the number of inbound
            transmission units that contained errors preventing them
            from being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 15 }

slot16ModuleifInFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 16 }

slot16ModuleifInUnknownProtos OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of packets
            received via the interface which were discarded because of
            an unknown or unsupported protocol.  For character-oriented
            or fixed-length interfaces that support protocol
            multiplexing the number of transmission units received via
            the interface which were discarded because of an unknown or
            unsupported protocol.  For any interface that does not
            support protocol multiplexing, this counter will always be
            0.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 17 }

slot16ModuleifOutOctets OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of octets transmitted out of the
            interface, including framing characters.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 18 }

slot16ModuleifOutUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were not addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 19 }

slot16ModuleifOutNUcastPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The total number of packets that higher-level protocols
            requested be transmitted, and which were addressed to a
            multicast or broadcast address at this sub-layer, including
            those that were discarded or not sent.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime.

            This object is deprecated in favour of ifOutMulticastPkts
            and ifOutBroadcastPkts."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 20 }

slot16ModuleifOutDiscards OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The number of outbound packets which were chosen to be
            discarded even though no errors had been detected to prevent
            their being transmitted.  One possible reason for discarding
            such a packet could be to free up buffer space.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 21 }

slot16ModuleifOutErrors OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "For packet-oriented interfaces, the number of outbound
            packets that could not be transmitted because of errors.
            For character-oriented or fixed-length interfaces, the
            number of outbound transmission units that could not be
            transmitted because of errors.

            Discontinuities in the value of this counter can occur at
            re-initialization of the management system, and at other
            times as indicated by the value of
            ifCounterDiscontinuityTime."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 22 }

slot16ModuleifOutFcsErrorPkts OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "FCS error pakets."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 23 }

slot16ModuleifOutQLen OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Gauge32
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      deprecated
    DESCRIPTION
            "The length of the output packet queue (in packets)."
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 24 }

slot16ModuleifOutOctetsRate OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX      Counter64
    MAX-ACCESS  read-only
    STATUS      current
    DESCRIPTION
            "The speed of octets trans on the interface(kbps)"
    ::= { slot16ModuleIfEntry 25 }

-- The boardPortManagement group --   
-- boardPortManagement --
boardInfoTable OBJECT-TYPE
     SYNTAX      SEQUENCE OF BoardInfoEntry
     MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
     STATUS      current
     DESCRIPTION
             "A list of all boards's information."
     ::= { boardPortManagement 1 }   
    
boardInfoEntry OBJECT-TYPE
     SYNTAX      BoardInfoEntry
     MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
     STATUS      current
     DESCRIPTION
             "An entry contains a board's information."
     INDEX   { statusChanged }
     ::= { boardInfoTable 1 } 

BoardInfoEntry ::= 
    SEQUENCE {    
                 statusChanged       DisplayString
     }   
    
statusChanged OBJECT-TYPE
     SYNTAX  DisplayString (SIZE (0..255))
     MAX-ACCESS  read-only
     STATUS      current
     DESCRIPTION
             "Board running status."
     ::= { boardInfoEntry 1 } 

-- traps --

linkProtectStatusChanged NOTIFICATION-TYPE
    STATUS  current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A link protect status changed trap signifies that the SNMP entity,
            acting in an agent role, has detected that the status
            is about to be changed."
    ::= { traps 1 }

cpuStatusChanged NOTIFICATION-TYPE
    STATUS  current
    DESCRIPTION
            "A cpu status change trap signifies that the SNMP entity,
            acting in an agent role, has detected that the cpu 
            status is about to be changed."
    ::= { traps 2 }

    STATUS  current
    DESCRIPTION
